25/07/21, 12:12 pm - Person2: package labprogram15;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.FileReader;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;

public class Exercise15a {
	public static void main(String[] args)
	{
		try
		{
			FileReader a1 = new FileReader("C:\\Users\\N PUNNIYA MURTHY\\Desktop\\hello.txt");
			BufferedReader a2 = new BufferedReader(a1);
			FileWriter a3 = new FileWriter("C:\\Users\\N PUNNIYA MURTHY\\Desktop\\hellocopy.txt", true);
			String s;
			while((s = a2.readLine()) != null)
			{
				a3.write(s);
			}
			a2.close();
			a3.close();
			System.out.println("File Has Been Copied Successfully");
		}
		catch(IOException e)
		{
			System.out.println(e);
		}
	}
}

			System.out.println("File Size is " + a1.length());
		}
		else
		{
			System.out.println("The file does not exist");
		}
	}

//Write a java program to demonstrate Array ListClass, LinkedList Class,TreeSet Class

import java.util.*;
class Book1
{
	int id;
	String name, author;
	//constructor
	Book1(int i, String n, String a)
	{
		id = i;
		name = n;
		author = a;
	}
	void display()
	{
		System.out.println("Book detail: " + id + " " + name + " " + author);
	}
}
public class Exercise16b 
{
	public static void main(String[] args)
	{
		Book1 b1 = new Book1(1, "C", " NIKITHA");
		Book1 b2 = new Book1(2, "C++", " LETHISHAA");
		Book1 b3 = new Book1(3, "Java", " JESTIN");
		Book1 b4 = new Book1(4, "Software Engineering", " SANDEEP");
		Book1 b5 = new Book1(5, "Dtat Structure", " SUNIL");
		Book1 b6 = new Book1(6, "Chemistry", " GLADWIN");
		
		//Syntax for linked list
		LinkedList<Book1> a1 = new LinkedList<Book1>();
		
		a1.add(b2);
		a1.add(b4);
		a1.add(b5);
		a1.addFirst(b3);
		a1.addLast(b1);
		
		for(Book1 a2:a1)
		{
			a2.display();
		}
		System.out.println("List the size : " + a1.size() + " \n ");
		
		if(a1.contains(b5))
		{
			System.out.println("Index of Book B5 is : " + a1.indexOf(b5));
		}
		else
		{
			System.out.println("\n data not found");
		}
		a1.add(5, b6);
		for(Book1 a2:a1)
		{
			a2.display();
		}
	}

}
25/07/21, 12:12 pm - Person2: package labprogram16;
//16a ArrayList class program
import java.util.*;
class Book
{
	int id;
	String name, author;
	
	Book(int i, String n, String a)
	{
		id = i;
		name = n;
		author = a;
	}
	void show()
	{
		System.out.println("Book Information: " + id + " " + name + " " + author); 
	}
}
public class Exercise16a 
{
	public static void main(String[] args)
	{
		Book b1 = new Book(123, "C", "JESTIN");
		Book b2 = new Book(124, "C++", "RICKY");
		Book b3 = new Book(125, "Java", "ASHER");
		
		//Syntax for ArrayList Class
		ArrayList<Book> a1 = new ArrayList<Book>();
		a1.add(b1);
		a1.add(b2);
		a1.add(b3);
		//System.out.println(a1);
		Iterator i1 = a1.iterator();
		while(i1.hasNext()) 
		{
			Book b4 = (Book)i1.next();
			b4.show();
		}
		Book b5 = a1.get(1);
		b5.show();
	}
}

//Write a java program to perform the basic TreeSet Class operation using Collection classes.

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class Exercise16c 
{
	public static void main(String[] args)
	{
		//syntax for TreeSet
		TreeSet<String> t1 = new TreeSet<String>();
		t1.add("CSE");
		t1.add("ISE");
		t1.add("MECH");
		
		System.out.println("Elements : " + t1);
		System.out.println("Check the Set is Empty : " + t1.isEmpty());
		
		//t1.clear();
		System.out.println("The siz of the set is : " + t1.size());
		
		t1.remove("MECH");
		System.out.println("Elements : " + t1);
		String[] s1 = {"Auto", "Bio", "CSE", "ISE", "CIVIL", "MECH", "ECE", "EEE"};
		List<String> l1 = Arrays.asList(s1);
		TreeSet<String> t2 = new TreeSet<String>(l1);
		System.out.println(t2);
	}
}
